This was announced yesterday by the operator of the Stuttgart Stock Exchange. The developer was her unit Sowa Labs.\nüîΩ It is noted that at the moment the novelty is available only to users from Germany, but in the future it will spread to other countries. For the time being, traders will be able to use Bison daily only from 6 am local time until midnight. In the Stuttgart Stock Exchange noted that the application has a news feed that uses artificial intelligence. In addition, users do not need to set up a wallet for trading. This is due to the fact that a subsidiary of Boerse Stuttgart - Blocknox, acts as a repository for users of the application, using the escrow system.\n‚ÄúHead of Sowa Labs, Ulli Spankowski, said that developers are planning to make money on price spreads.‚Äù Blocknox, another division of the Stuttgart Stock Exchange, will be responsible for storing the assets. application, through which users can use the functions of the wallet without connecting to a computer.\n‚úÖThe application called Ledger Live was previously only available for personal computers, but now it has been launched for mobile devices. With it, users of the new wallet Ledger Nano X will be able to use all the functions of the wallet using a Bluetooth connection.\nRepresentatives of the company noted that at the moment the application is targeted specifically at users of Ledger Nano X, but the owners of Nano S and Blue can only check the balance on their device. In the future, however, users of old models will also be able to use all the functions of the device from a mobile phone. For Nano S, you will have to use an OTG USB adapter, and all functions will be available only on Android OS.\n‚ùóÔ∏è Note that the interface of the Ledger application is very similar to that of a competitor, Trezor Bridge, which was released last year. However, all the functionality of Trezor devices is available only on personal computers, and only a limited list of operations can be performed from a mobile phone.\n‚òù Recall that at the end of last year, at the 35C3 Refreshing Memories conference, researchers announced the possibility of hacking into the hardware wallets Ledger Nano S and Ledger Blue. (USD) Daily Future‚Äù and will cost 1 BTC. The contract will be calculated in US dollars. The minimum price fluctuation will be $ 2.50 for one contract; however, for large transactions from ten contracts, it will be possible to determine the price with an accuracy of up to $ 0.01. There are no daily restrictions on price fluctuations, but a limit of 100,000 lots has been set. Commission for exchange and clearing services will be $ 0.50 for each participant in the transaction.\nFor the purpose of technical implementation of trade, listing of new contracts will be held every day. Trading will be conducted from 8:00 pm to 6:00 pm the following day, New York time. Preliminary opening of the auction will be carried out at 19:55, and calculations will be made from 16:58 to 17:00.\nüîΩ Obviously, the Bakkt platform is ready to start trading, but has to wait for permission from the US Commodity Futures Trading Commission (CFTC). security problems‚ùóÔ∏è\n‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è‚ö°Ô∏è\n The long-awaited update of Constantinople Ethereum was postponed after a critical vulnerability was discovered in one of the planned changes. The company ChainSecurity, which is engaged in the audit of smart contracts, said on Tuesday that the proposal to improve Ethereum (EIP) No. 1283, if implemented, could provide an attacker with a loophole in the code to steal users' funds.\n‚úÖDuring the teleconference, Ethereum developers, as well as client developers and other network projects, agreed to postpone hardfork for at least as long as they evaluate the problem. Among the participants of the teleconference were the creator of Ethereum Vitalik Buterin, the developers Hudson Jameson, Nick Johnson and Evan Van Ness, as well as the product manager Parity Afri Schoedon.\n–ëWhen discussing the vulnerability, the project developers came to the conclusion that the correction of the error will take too much time and cannot be implemented before the hard forks, which was scheduled for 04:00 UTC on January 17th. The new date of the hardfork will be determined during the regular teleconference of Ethereum developers on Friday.\n‚òù A vulnerability called a re-entry attack allows an attacker to re-access the same function several times without informing the user. Last week, the exchange has already added support for perpetual swaps on BCH, so 4 types of such contracts are now available on it.\nPerpetual swaps operate on the principle of futures contracts, but with unlimited validity and the possibility of closing at any time. Swaps allow traders to open both short and long positions, speculating on the dynamic of the course.\n‚úÖ For BCH, ETH and EOS swaps, a leverage ratio of up to 40x is available. In addition, each contract is equivalent to $ 10. To determine the price of swaps, data from several exchanges are used. Traders can leverage up to 100x, and the value of such a contract is $ 100.\nOK About OKEx plans to add new perpetual contracts became known in early December. Then it was assumed that they will be available from December 11. in ICO-projects\nüî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•\nThe State Duma is planning to introduce a limit on private investment, which is directed to various projects, including cryptoactive assets, RBC reports.\nüîΩAccording to the draft law on the regulation of crowdfunding platforms, which is being prepared for consideration by the State Duma, individuals who do not have the status of a qualified investor will be allowed to invest no more than 600 thousand rubles a year in crowdfunding projects with the condition that investments in one project should not exceed 100 thousand rubles. It clarifies the Central Bank, to invest more than 600 thousand rubles a year will be possible only to persons who have received the status of a qualified investor in accordance with the law \"On the Securities Market.\"\nüî∫ ‚ÄúInvesting through crowdfunding (investment) platforms is high-risk and may lead to the loss of all invested funds in full. With the aim of accepting such risks by unqualified investors, a limit on the volume of investment during one year is introduced to no more than 600 thousand rubles, ‚Äùexplain the representatives of the Bank of Russia.\nThis innovation directly affects ICO-projects that are associated with the release of digital assets. The amount indicated by the State Duma is extremely small, say representatives of the Russian Association of Cryptoindustry and Blockchain (RACIB), because usually the average private investor can invest about 1-3 million rubles a year into an ICO project using crowdfunding sites. That is why the association suggested that officials set a limit of 2 million rubles instead of 600 thousand rubles.\nThe draft law on the regulation of crowdfunding üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•üî•\n #ICO #–≥–æ—Å–¥—É–º–∞ #–†–æ—Å—Å–∏—è #–∫—Ä–∞—É–¥—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥–∏–Ω–≥ #–†–ê–ö–ò–ë #–†–ë–ö",

launch of smart assets and smart accounts in the core network.\nSmart assets enable Waves users to apply different scripts to tokens. These scripts validate transactions for smart assets before adding them to the blockchain.\n–°–º–∞—Ä—ÇSmart assets can be used for the following purposes:\n- freezing of assets (implies blocking a token before a block with a certain height is reached);\n- ‚Äúblack / white lists‚Äù, which allow or prohibit the sending of tokens to certain addresses;\n- setting commissions;\n- multi-signature transactions;\n- control over trading pairs, which allows you to exchange tokens for predetermined assets.\n‚ùóÔ∏èThe developers also note that the new functionality can be used in a wide variety of user cases and can be useful both to business structures and individual users.\nüîΩSmart accounts, according to representatives of the Waves Platform, are Turing-incomplete smart contracts that allow you to execute code on the blockchain, but with the stipulated restrictions on functionality. These limitations avoid unwanted usage scenarios and help improve system reliability.\nSmart accounts can be used for different operations with tokens. The list of functions includes: accounts with multi-signatures, atomic swaps, freezing of tokens, two-factor authentication, white list voting and data oracles.\n‚òù Note that for the implementation of smart accounts used programming language RIDE, developed by the creators of Waves. It supports operations with Ether, ERC-20 and ERC-721 standards tokens, as well as Ethereum-dapp operation. Opera decided to introduce support for Ethereum solutions, as they considered that the community of developers of decentralized applications on this network is the largest.\n‚ùóÔ∏èAs Opera Crypto product manager Charles Hamel points out, if earlier online use of cryptocurrencies and access to Web 3 required special applications or extensions, now this inconvenience has been eliminated. Also, thanks to the feedback received, the stability of the browser and its compatibility with dapp has been improved.\n‚ÄúNo extensions and applications need to be installed.
